1. restaurant style Quinoa power bowl — Fluffy quinoa with roasted chickpeas and lemon-tahini drizzle. Prepared by: Rinse 1 cup quinoa under cold water until clear.. Bring 2 cups water to a boil, add quinoa, cover and simmer on low for 15 minutes.. Drain chickpeas, pat dry. Toss with olive oil, paprika, salt. Roast at 400°F for 20 min.. Dice cucumber, halve tomatoes, slice avocado. Whisk tahini with lemon juice and salt.. Fluff quinoa with a fork. Build bowl: quinoa, chickpeas, veggies, tahini dressing, parsley. Served with quinoa, chickpeas, cucumber, cherry tomatoes, avocado, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

2. restaurant style Teriyaki salmon bowl — Wild-caught salmon glazed with teriyaki over brown rice and broccoli. Prepared by: Mix tamari, honey, grated ginger, and minced garlic for the teriyaki glaze.. Cook brown rice per package directions, about 35–40 minutes.. Pat salmon dry, season. Cook skin-side up 3 min, flip, add glaze, cook 3 more.. Steam broccoli 4 minutes until bright green and tender-crisp.. Build bowl: rice, salmon, broccoli, edamame. Spoon glaze over. Sprinkle sesame seeds. Served with salmon fillet, brown rice, broccoli, edamame, tamari, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

3. restaurant style Veggie egg white frittata — Light egg white frittata packed with colorful vegetables. Prepared by: Preheat oven to 375°F. Separate 8 eggs, season whites and whisk until frothy.. Dice bell pepper, slice mushrooms, mince garlic. Sauté in olive oil 4 minutes.. Add spinach, stir until wilted. Spread veggies evenly across the pan.. Pour egg whites over veggies. Scatter tomatoes and feta. Cook on stovetop 2 minutes.. Bake 10–12 minutes until center is firm and lightly golden. Served with egg whites, spinach, bell pepper, mushrooms, cherry tomatoes, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

4. restaurant style Turkey lettuce tacos — Lean turkey in crisp butter lettuce cups with avocado. Prepared by: Separate butter lettuce into large cup-shaped leaves.. Dice avocado, mince jalapeño, chop cilantro. Mix with lime juice and a pinch of salt.. Cook ground turkey in a hot skillet, breaking apart, until no pink remains, 6–7 min.. Add cumin, chili powder, diced tomatoes, and a squeeze of lime. Cook 2 more minutes.. Spoon turkey into lettuce cups. Top with avocado mixture and extra cilantro. Served with ground turkey, butter lettuce, avocado, lime, jalapeño, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

5. restaurant style Red lentil soup — Warming spiced lentil soup with coconut milk and turmeric. Prepared by: Dice onion, mince garlic, grate ginger. Sauté onion in oil 5 minutes until soft.. Add garlic, ginger, turmeric, cumin, and coriander. Stir 1 minute until fragrant.. Add rinsed lentils and vegetable broth. Bring to a boil then reduce to a simmer.. Simmer uncovered 15 minutes until lentils are completely soft.. Stir in coconut milk and lemon juice. Season with salt. Simmer 5 more minutes. Served with red lentils, coconut milk, vegetable broth, turmeric, cumin, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

6. restaurant style Chickpea shawarma wrap — Crispy spiced chickpeas with hummus in a whole wheat wrap. Prepared by: Drain, rinse, and pat chickpeas dry. Toss with olive oil, paprika, garlic powder, turmeric, salt.. Roast chickpeas at 425°F for 20–25 minutes until crispy.. Slice cucumber, dice tomato, shred red cabbage.. Warm tortilla in a dry skillet 30 seconds per side.. Spread hummus on tortilla. Layer veggies then crispy chickpeas. Wrap tightly. Served with chickpeas, whole wheat tortilla, hummus, cucumber, tomato, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

7. restaurant style Greek chicken mason jar salad — Grilled chicken with olives, feta, and lemon-oregano dressing. Prepared by: Season chicken with salt, pepper, oregano, and olive oil. Cook in a grill pan 5–6 min per side.. Rest chicken 5 minutes then slice against the grain.. Whisk olive oil, lemon juice, oregano, salt, and pepper for the dressing.. Layer jar: dressing, olives, cucumber, tomatoes, red onion, feta, chicken, romaine on top.. Seal and refrigerate up to 3 days. Shake to dress and eat straight from the jar. Served with chicken breast, romaine, kalamata olives, cucumber, red onion, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

8. restaurant style Zucchini noodle pad thai — Spiralized zucchini with shrimp and a tangy peanut sauce. Prepared by: Spiralize 2 zucchinis. Salt lightly and let sit on paper towels 10 minutes.. Whisk peanut butter, tamari, lime juice, honey, and warm water into a smooth sauce.. Sear shrimp in a hot wok 1–2 min per side until pink. Remove and set aside.. Scramble 2 eggs in the same pan until just set. Push to the side.. Add zucchini noodles and sauce. Toss on high heat 2 minutes. Return shrimp, add bean sprouts, plate with scallions and peanuts. Served with zucchini, shrimp, eggs, peanut butter, tamari, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

9. restaurant style Overnight oats with berries — No-cook oats with chia seeds, berries, and almond butter. Prepared by: Add ½ cup rolled oats and 1 tbsp chia seeds to a mason jar.. Pour in ¾ cup almond milk, ½ tsp vanilla, and 1 tsp honey. Stir well.. Dollop 3 tbsp Greek yogurt. Seal and refrigerate at least 6 hours or overnight.. In the morning, slice strawberries and banana. Give oats a stir.. Top with blueberries, strawberries, banana, and a drizzle of almond butter. Served with rolled oats, almond milk, chia seeds, blueberries, strawberries, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

10. restaurant style Lemon herb baked chicken — Juicy oven-baked chicken thighs with garlic, lemon, and rosemary. Prepared by: Preheat oven to 425°F. Pat chicken thighs dry.. Mix olive oil, lemon zest, lemon juice, minced garlic, Dijon, rosemary, thyme, salt, and pepper.. Coat chicken all over with marinade. Let sit 10 minutes at room temperature.. Place chicken skin-side up in a baking dish. Roast 25–30 minutes until skin is golden.. Rest 5 minutes before serving. Spoon pan juices over the top. Served with chicken thighs, lemon, garlic, rosemary, thyme, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

11. restaurant style Asian lettuce wraps — Savory ground chicken with water chestnuts in crisp lettuce cups. Prepared by: Mince garlic, grate ginger, dice water chestnuts and mushrooms.. Heat sesame oil in a wok. Brown ground chicken, breaking apart, 5 minutes.. Add garlic, ginger, mushrooms, and water chestnuts. Stir-fry 3 minutes.. Add tamari, hoisin, and a splash of water. Toss to coat and cook 1 more minute.. Spoon filling into lettuce cups. Top with scallions and serve immediately. Served with ground chicken, butter lettuce, water chestnuts, shiitake mushrooms, tamari, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

12. restaurant style Broccoli cheddar egg muffins — Portable egg muffins loaded with broccoli and sharp cheddar. Prepared by: Preheat oven to 375°F. Grease a 12-cup muffin tin well with olive oil.. Finely chop broccoli and red onion. Steam broccoli 2 minutes until just tender.. Whisk 8 eggs with 2 tbsp milk, salt, pepper, and garlic powder.. Divide broccoli and onion among muffin cups. Pour egg mixture over. Sprinkle cheddar.. Bake 18–20 minutes until puffed and set. Cool 5 minutes before removing. Served with eggs, broccoli, sharp cheddar, red onion, salt, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

13. restaurant style Chicken tikka masala lite — Lighter version of the classic with Greek yogurt marinade. Prepared by: Cut chicken into chunks. Marinate in Greek yogurt, garam masala, cumin, turmeric, garlic, ginger for 20 min.. Cook marinated chicken in a hot skillet until charred in spots, about 6–8 minutes. Set aside.. In the same pan, sauté diced onion 5 minutes. Add garlic and ginger, cook 1 minute.. Add canned tomatoes and remaining spices. Simmer 10 minutes until thickened.. Return chicken. Simmer 5 minutes. Finish with cilantro and serve. Served with chicken breast, Greek yogurt, canned tomatoes, onion, garlic, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

14. restaurant style Tuna avocado rice bowl — Sushi-inspired bowl with seasoned tuna and creamy avocado. Prepared by: Season cooked rice with rice vinegar and a pinch of salt while still warm.. Drain tuna well. Mix with tamari, sesame oil, and a dash of sriracha.. Slice avocado and cucumber into thin pieces.. Build the bowl: seasoned rice, tuna, avocado, cucumber, torn nori.. Sprinkle sesame seeds and drizzle extra sriracha or tamari to taste. Served with canned tuna, cooked rice, avocado, cucumber, tamari, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

16. restaurant style Sheet pan turkey meatballs — Lean turkey meatballs roasted on one pan with marinara. Prepared by: Preheat oven to 400°F. Mix turkey, breadcrumbs, egg, minced garlic, Italian seasoning, salt.. Roll into golf ball-sized balls and place on a lined baking sheet.. Drizzle with olive oil and bake 18–20 minutes until browned.. Warm marinara in a saucepan. Add meatballs and simmer together 5 minutes.. Garnish with Parmesan and fresh parsley. Serve with zucchini noodles. Served with ground turkey, breadcrumbs, egg, garlic, Italian seasoning, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

17. restaurant style Moroccan carrot soup — Velvety spiced carrot soup with harissa and a coconut cream swirl. Prepared by: Dice onion, mince garlic, peel and chop carrots. Grate fresh ginger.. Sauté onion in oil 5 minutes. Add garlic, ginger, cumin, and coriander. Cook 1 minute.. Add carrots and broth. Bring to a boil, reduce and simmer 20 minutes until very tender.. Blend until completely smooth.. Stir in harissa and lemon juice. Swirl coconut cream on top and serve. Served with carrots, onion, garlic, vegetable broth, coconut cream, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

Season with salt and pepper.. Mix chopped parsley, lemon zest, minced garlic, breadcrumbs, capers, and olive oil.. Press gremolata firmly onto the top of each cod fillet.. Bake 12–15 minutes until fish flakes easily with a fork.. Squeeze fresh lemon over the top and serve with roasted asparagus. Served with cod fillets, parsley, lemon, garlic, olive oil, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

Assemble bowl: cauliflower rice, beans, corn, pico, avocado. Finish with lime and cilantro. Served with black beans, cauliflower rice, corn, red bell pepper, avocado, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

Cook 2–3 minutes until bubbles form on the surface and edges look set. Flip gently.. Cook 1–2 minutes on the second side. Serve with blueberries, almond butter, and maple syrup. 33. restaurant style Baked falafel bowl — Crispy baked falafel over rice with tahini and fresh herbs. Form into small patties.. Place patties on an oiled baking sheet. Brush tops with olive oil. Bake at 425°F for 25 min, flipping halfway.. Whisk tahini with lemon juice, garlic, and water until smooth and pourable.. Serve falafel over brown rice with tahini sauce, fresh parsley, diced tomato and cucumber. Add cumin, chili powder, smoked paprika, and salt. Stir 1 minute.. Add a splash of chicken broth to moisten. Stir and cook 1 more minute.. Cool completely before dividing into 4 airtight containers. Refrigerate 4 days. Served with ground turkey, onion, garlic, cumin, chili powder, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

206. restaurant style Roasted vegetable prep — Sheet pan of roasted mixed vegetables to use all week. Prepared by: Preheat oven to 425°F. Line two large baking sheets with parchment.. Chop all vegetables into similar 1-inch pieces.. Toss vegetables with olive oil, garlic, Italian seasoning, salt, and pepper.. Spread in a single layer across both sheets. Roast 20–22 minutes, rotating once.. Cool completely. Divide into 5 airtight containers. Refrigerate up to 5 days. Served with zucchini, bell peppers, red onion, broccoli, cherry tomatoes, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

207. restaurant style Teriyaki chicken prep — Batch teriyaki chicken for bowls and salads throughout the week. Prepared by: Mix tamari, honey, garlic, ginger, sesame oil, and rice vinegar for the teriyaki marinade.. Cook 4 chicken thighs in an oven-safe skillet over medium-high, 4 min per side.. Pour teriyaki sauce over chicken. Transfer skillet to 375°F oven. Bake 15 minutes.. Rest chicken 5 minutes. Slice and divide into 4 meal prep containers.. Serve over cooked brown rice with sesame seeds and scallions. Refrigerate up to 4 days. Served with chicken thighs, tamari, honey, garlic, ginger, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

Served with mixed greens, romaine lettuce, kale, cucumber, carrots, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

209. restaurant style Chickpea and vegetable curry prep — Big-batch chickpea curry for 5 days of satisfying lunches. Prepared by: Sauté diced onion in oil 5 minutes until golden.. Add garlic, ginger, cumin, garam masala, and turmeric. Cook 1 minute.. Add canned tomatoes. Simmer 8 minutes until thickened.. Add chickpeas and coconut milk. Simmer 10 minutes.. Stir in spinach until wilted. Cool. Divide into 5 containers. Refrigerate 4 days. Served with chickpeas, spinach, canned tomatoes, onion, garlic, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2

210. restaurant style Hard-boiled eggs x12 — A dozen perfect hard-boiled eggs for the whole week. Prepared by: Place 12 eggs in a single layer in a large saucepan. Cover with cold water by 1 inch.. Bring to a full boil over medium-high heat. Reduce to medium-low.. Simmer exactly 10 minutes for fully set yolks.. Transfer immediately to an ice bath. Let cool 15 minutes.. Peel or refrigerate unpeeled up to 1 week. Season to taste when eating. Served with eggs, water, salt, ice, black pepper, professional food photography, natural lighting, overhead shot, --ar 3:2
